giyagni tunkakno wa yineru tokanu pirana wixako wtokanumka wumatinitkalo kiruka wchinkaka wixa
gi pejnu kakwalupa gixeta
gigkaklu gi wa gotslu seyni rumatjemko
ga wa xani tye gogne gwashlu wumatatkalu kajine gimatkale
suxo gimtugachro koxa gi gimkata jirgaleta girixanu tumkata gimtukletlu kakwalupa rujpaganuna
gi rixa wane wixjetanu
gi pejnu gagaje pumkata kamruretyalu payaglukaka
kluneru gapni satkaka shimagapi
gi wa gixo magatatka nikatyapluna wa rustajregapna satni yinerni wane gajerni katsotu giwakatletachrini mapa myoji rustaknanwa poyagnukta wanenanru satu kshana gimatachri wale gipxakamyojitlu kapaygonro kchiyma ga wa kshimunayma wanepnute ranikluna pinrewatikowakapji
satu chalu kamlewatanu nuru chalugatyapa
giyaka garoso tenekanno nyegwaklo kachiperpotni
tunatka noturu yimakjero giyagni rumuwata
gowukako retgimatlu kshoteru nukojiru giwa rumkata giylaletlu
giwa nkegeknanuwatanu mturune giknogatkalu kyapreru kamrurchi
gaxawripane wyantatanu ramgagetkotanatkana kapetgogne
koshma saxpatkoklunpatka ginkakanunno nalukgetleta numatkamruretyaplu

topapkotkani tapokinri nunko tkamrurewatyawakaya
kamrureko rawa nyegwaklu giyako salwayegitanatkano
gipimkata yangaletno nunro girixanu nupxakgognenatyi ptowruko
gepchiyma rustaklu chichmuna natjiru kapetgogne
meyiwlekakna rapokna nwugenene xani nagajetannatkana rumgognenatna
kigle rixyaplu panchi pganuru pupxakanunru nomole
mshinikanutu rixle gikeko galukanru yinerni

msaplo katu patkanwa koseryegitannatkawu giwa wumata pguta

namanutanatka shimanepje niikanatka garosmaka naluknikletanatka
gosha yinitka poyoliri retgimamtatkalu gatnugapoya gixo knoyane

giswajiyegikakaya pushyajetanu giwa jiglokyapa gonu gina rixinipa
panchi kamrutyalona suxo tupnagnurutana gike gipxakanatkalo
ragyekana shiji wutakleni xani rumtutewnanuna
nuru pupxakakanru nyegwaklu retashanata giyaka rupxaklewata sanaya
kigleru rupxakyawu wutsrukate tengogne gajeru gipagogneko ramtakwu
powrapotutlunajejine rapga rushpakyapa kanawatsigi rapogatinipa
jimeka wutaka sanaya goyechnokawpotuko wushpaka tumananu wsatokanu
gita girukotanru yayixachri gipjiya goyechnokawpotuko nyayegitanru
ramgagimamtyana tsapane nukojirni yagapgatini kapetgoggne
klunerukokta rugitanu natjiru repomginipluna wupokchi pirana
kaynuto tanjitlu tukojiru nshicho seyni chipetyanro

pachiji ragjita nyegwaklu ganna rutakyawakapa
gixo shima rawinna natjirune rapiknona xani getko gikeko rawapanna
girixa giwa pganuruwatatka pkagwakluge pganuru nshicho petashatanutkalu
giwa ramanutna jejine supawgajene kamrurewatinna gichkolunni
gerotu kojitkaka ranika nyegwaklu reneksatyapna yine

kapetgogne wetanatna yenewatachine kaypotuko wsatokana

pugletanru pkanawate nepuru kiglepotu wixyaplu retsotanatanunna pimrine
kiglepotlu shiji gipchekachri wyonakanutkalu wusanate

nepuro kshinikanuro tixinripa pshicho puykotanro giwa petashatanro
ginna nwenutanu yonaykyawakna chinanu china naganuru

yayixana makluji kgalixkolni xani yayixpotutanatka kegeknanuwatana
pejnuruko shiji gimretkota ma nikyaplu kochi
nyegwaklo wuynumsagiwakatanru wepuru jemyapwu gapatluya

yineryonga wyonatini getpotutanu giwa wumtukanru

pushinkapanru psoluko gigkakletkarurupa rumatjemyapyina yine jemachinepa
gewi rasukyatka yineru giylalewatachri ginakaktayatka
kayatu jrinakotkani wa kewe natjiru puratanru pejnuruneko yine getlu
kapchopotlu mshiri gerkayatanutkalu nwugenene kananutkalu
mgenoklu gitsruka ruylata natjiru goshaya
yine mshinikanune giylatanru wumolni kapetgogne gipjiya
mkachrisama genekashatikolu gerkanutka xani nwugenene gitakanrupa
nyegwaklo nalnamtatka napokinipa ntomsatanyi
giwa runawa jeji tsapitachripa mamernuwgetkota
potukle wutaklu sawli mawamtakyaplu sana wyinipa
wkayitana wutkaplu runroyegi nustaplole tchina nomeknajiro
pkagwakanunno nganunro ragjigapkatanu nepuru ginkalu ragjitawa
wnikatanru girkaluru gikeko wsaletanu wyaprekamruretanruni
waneko rixgognenatna gimetachine wupokchiya ruylakakjetna koya rurinna
tsrushkikitkani mikili kapetgogne netlu nsalwatapini
xani tuna nomekagyo noturu giwa puylakanunro petwamonutanunro
nikchinepni ranikanu poyoliri gosha yatka goyechnokawpotuko
nshiretanu yopkamtkotka gagajekaka panchi kamrutyapna
mama saga gojitanro wa numwatsitanro tumtuwnana
kgimatkalerni yongatachri giyagni pejnuruneko yayegitlu rupxakyapna
petashatanru puturu raprintitanru giynumsagkaklu gike yokwityaplu
gatnugapoya rumugkaklewkakananumtna maklujine galukakachine
nsaplo pumuynumsakakanu puturu kampukjeruyma patewatana
pugkakanru nuru ranikamtanru psoluko kiruka wkamrunatanru pokchi pirana
rumuwpotuta retyaglutinitkana wugenene natjiru
susawotikowaka putakanru gixosure girixanu magatanu pinrine yine chinanupa
gi raluka pinregetna yinni kpinrewakleru rumtuwnashatatka
rasukamta noturu rugkakyapwu rapokyawaka wutsrukate pagixankaka ranika
xani gipegnu walapu xani waneylu nomekagyi nalukgetletatkalu
penekanno pyaglu naganuru potuklepotu nupxakanru wupjiya
xako ruylatyanaplu wakate natjirni numwastsitanru
yoyechno kamalampi ruranatna kagonchine shikalwanatna
gerkajetkalurni namchi powraygi wixyapa
xani wupekotlu gitsrukachi pejnuroko sroshchi renekyawu rumuwata
giwa kamnixka yineru mshinikanutu puykotanunru nyegwaklo
gaxawripane takaka nsaplo serolgawni niika xani klu serolga tkamrutinitka
niika gichkapitanna mgenoklu gaxawripanni kapetgogne
tsrushkikine rixinitkana jejine gikeko rumkatatkana mturune pixka rixatkana
koygaklerno giyagni ginmagatya jimeka koya tkamrutyapa nganunro
gigetko galikakni rugkakyawuna pokchi gajene ginriklo wyinri giwa ralpokotna
nomolene nugkakapgi getapyaplu papa yayixanatka kegeknanuwatana
wanemkalu koya seyni kapsatkalu waleko nutangi nomolene
nshicho nalukanropotu yayixyanno nwamonuwata
rukshikyatkalu noturu ruru kanawate xani rumuwatanu nugkakanru
klunge giklukanru wa maklujni kastikatanruna pejnuruneko suxone
nikaluru putakamtinna ma nachichyapna mturune jiglokyawakna
giwa nugleretlu gektutu piranalu giyagni gikeko napoka gita
jiro pugkakanru totu kamruptogitanutnakluna katsluje
nugleretpotutlu shimagle seyni pakatkaka numkatana girixanu nkamrurewatana
rumatyempotutanatkalo nganuru wa nshichni taluka gasuktatletini
rayokgimatatkalo ganunro nepuru tumtuwnagognenata
nshicho tkagwakatkayi pupxalo pshiretanutka kayi gapokannatka njiglokyawaka
katni wa giylapratanno tchinna najiro tomekaginni xani nachichotanungi
sato kanawa kamturinri nganuru noturu rumuwpotuta
pejnuruneko yine wugkakanu gayinripa seyni wshirtapanu
kanawakta yognika mturu pugkakanru ruru rawapyaplu seyo nkowchogatinrini
tugleyoptolgimatlu nsaplo wa tganuru tkagwakanatanrutkani
yinuwakiniwa gapatlu wapoka wjempotuta chinyawaka pogirchi
lamas pokchi tyagapgata najiro natjiruyma
kpinrewaklero tomsatlu jeji tyoglotyaplu girixanu yayixana
santira ganikajite nenekanro mturo tnikinropa
kapetgogne kamgatkaluna gashgaji reneksashatyapna tsroshkikine
kshana sagatluna maklujni giyagni sepronana ginakakokta yashatana
tsru gapga yatkana nomolene kanawastsigi kamrurewtapanna
giwa nugleretlu rapatleya wale jeji xani nyangapanunru
gixo tantaygi gashkatanru nurni rusanateya kachinolewatanru
nepuro nuna koya nalukgirletana pshiretanu nonannugpotutana
gi palotonanni popnijiro wane getko twa sagita
petashtapanru pganuru nshicho giwa pyanganutkalu
giwa petwamonutanno seprolo pchinanrokgonrano njemjejetyi nomeknajiro

pshininampatkalu rapokinitkana pejnuruneko jejine shiji gitakapachine
rugkakanatno gitsrukachi retyawaka giwa kigle giwekle wixana
katu gnunro gonu gwapanu tchinna najiro toturune gitkoxni rawapinna
rapokatka pogirchi xani repomganutkana yine girixa giwa kagwakluna

waleko tganurutatka gimka ralukluna tomolene girixanu meretgimni

giwa wumata katgapkakta gapoka wupjiya kapetgogne

chiyagata mturu koshchekokluni ruglereta galpipotuta
yineryonga nyonyegitanu mkachrichratayegi misa wutakyapa
gitanu nkanawape panikanu nyegwaklu pchalugatapinipa
kigleru pirana chinyawaka pogirchi rumuwatna nomolene nopokchi gajene
najiro yimakanwu saxpalu giyagni goyechnokawpotuko tchanixwu topjiya
kapetgogne wungatkalu gitsrukachi yagapgagimatanu
tupnana mturni goyechno gishpakachroni tunro giylatanro
gi rixpokgapkatka koya wkamrutini naluka gimatleta
wale makluji raluka kashimyoletanro maklojni
rali giwlaletatkana ginrochine ponikgiwlalpotna
tomsatatkana gimekagine nuru rugkaklewyegityapna gipjiya
pumugkaklewkakanutka pejnurunekoyma suxone koya wkamrutyapa
nganuru panikanna pumolene wupokchi wumatyapna ginaka runyana
gita gimepe yonretanru kiruka rumtukanruna mturune
turu yokanatlo mturo paranta tanjityapa seyni tmamernuwata
tyegogne nsosagi tenkapno noyejewlo pimri tushagkapa gasokari tagjityapa
rapokatkana maklujine gatnugapoya gipxakachine koya wutagatanutkana
wuya katmaklege gipxakwu gixo shimane wkashicha wtuwumtatanutka
gixeko nikchi ruxeta kewe psoluko nikatlu xani klu nikanunna pimrine kewenni
sato kirukamtaji reneklo gitsrukachi wa nunro
gayanutka ruyolikyapna wganurune yechikawa wale gonra wnikanu
pejnuruneko yine getana tekakgisrutanna sixo gimetachro
nyegwaklu puynumsayegitanru wuru giwa rumatjematka
gixo mkachri ragjitapna yine pokchiya xani kwenu rixanruna gewi
psagatanrupotuko panikanutka yagluchi wekakgityapna pejnuruneko yine
kagwuru tuglereta makloji xani tyagapgatinipa tanikamtanu
muchinangapka wyanshinikanutanu nepuro klu wushagkanu kaykaka nopjiya
pshinitsogkaka tujretananumtyalo nyegwaklo wgenene nunro tumusalwatinna
tujrukatka mankowa wapatjetanro mturune nikanropa
tapokatka walentina goyechnokawpotuko gewi rutakamtlona
pochipujiru twapa najiro tshicho tenekyapa
giwa pyimakanutkana shikalchi gimatachinetka kanashkatanunwuna
gixo kashrine kamruta natjiru girixanu runrikapanna rapgaya
xani katjetka mturu rushpakiniyakawa seyni giwa yayixa
nsheyitanutkalu gishagkikowaka sawalgogne waneko gishagkini
xani tpuratlu kewe najiro seyni runanna twugenene wanna ganikininro
kiglepcheta rixanu rutakoklunuwa shiji nusanateya
pugkakanru yimaklewatachri rumatjemkakinripa
giwa paranta raluka pokowletna mamernuna rixyawakna wa maklujine
ginakakta gekakginatyatkana psoluko chiji wane rawanutkana pnuko ginyachine
pugkakpotutanno pejnuruneklege yagapgatanu yechikawa tsro kanawa wanjityapa wpoyagotyapa
rumaxiklewata gitsrukaachi gikta kamrurewatna maklujine
kapayni nikanata satu chkotuwgene katgetko grnrklu
gistakgaputikolu ruwshokgata mturu kapetgogne
klunerukokta pkamrujetanu giwa pyanshinikanutanutka nomole yatka pganuru
pochwajiru pwalojiru nalukana papikanunno nomeknajiro
wjiweta kapetgogne najiroyma numatatka xani nshicho nyimakanu
yawlo rawmanetna mshinikanune yine nopokchi gajene
rupnanatka wutsrukatni kshinikanurni wale wushinkapinri pagogne
ptomsatanru yineru wepomgiyaplu ginaka rutakamna pimrine yine
kokoo ginakyegii punanutka tumananustsitkani gemetkalu pamanutanuna
gimnuno tchinanru kamowa poyolirni goshaya
tumuwata mariya gerotumkalukta tutaka
xani tkagwakpirata nepuro tshiretanmakatka tamganata
jejine gosha gwanatachine gishpakatka kapetgogne
gi mshinikanuto nixiniko nopji nuwshokyaplu noturu
panikiniplu motoro muchinangapka yagotko giwa rumtukyapa
shiji gitakikolgapi penekanno nomekagyo gita shiretanu
pejnurgogne kayi tapokjeta suxo giyagni rumtuwnajeta tganuru
pugkakanru rugkaklewyegityapyawu nomeknatjiru giwa gapatlu wumkata yaletanuna
nopji yagotika mkachrikaka rumugansaletanrupna maklojine
pgimejiro rapatjetna pejnuruneko suxone nopokchiya
wchanixanna pejnuruneko yine sana wakamrutyapa rupxakanunwuna
rumutlo nuru nshicho girixanu ralukpotutlo ramtakjetlo tyagapgatini
gita teneka kayagoko pochwapagiru pinrine galikaka gixo teneka nsaplo
wale pixkalutukotnaka gistonrechi tanika nepuro xani
ptowrunanuko tanika nunro lima pokchiya nyegwaklo tsro tmagnantaka
kapetgognepnutgogne kegeknanuwatana nyegwakluni rupkatana klanko ragyeka
malasreta yigata noturu wamonuwata ganunro pogwakata
panikanru tsojritatga klunerukokta wane wumretanu
pyangaganro pshicho nyegwaklo giyagni tupxakagkoxyi tsalwashatatka
mugletu tonajine ruknoka kgishankaleru tye kayno
giglepoko kamruretanru wa panchi kigle getkotaa rixyapa
chpii tixa gepchipopeji tashkatinwu gimka tsronanukni
nyegwaklo tomsatno tugkakno ganikamtyaplu kowigaje
panikanru puturu pjiglokyawakaya gikeko getanunru pupjiya
runatkana solalone kashichyapluna yineru giylalewatachri
nustaplole pugkakanro punro retapanruna patjiru yayixgimatana
xani katu kamrutlu jimekapagi psojimka genekanunno gitkoxni
giwa nikanna yinni maleshatkani niikaluru
kochi gishale wukshika kapetgogne nopjiya
saplewamtana gaxawripawgenejini koshchekamtiniyakawlu pakcha
tujrukana mariya mture giyagni
mpomreto chininitkalo tganuru nyegwaklo tumtuwnapotuta tagajetanru ga wa tuwshokanru topjiya
mpomreto chinrona maklojni twamonuwatana chinyawaklona
gimka puylakanno nganuru pumtukgojitanno
gipji repomgiyatnaklu gituru nukojiru rasuktatyawaka
chko rujrukgatana noturni rapgaya chiyagatana girixanu giwa rumata ganogatana
giwa kigleru pokchi pyiyawaka wane rawna kagonchine mshinikanune
giwa taluka gimkakakletna nwugenen nunro nalukgansaletana
renekatkana nuru shiji gitakalurupa xani yanutkana jejine rutaklewtapanutkana
wuglepokotinwa watskopijete mawujrukyapa
giwa gitakashtkalurupni mkachrisama tchinwu wajiro njirukotanru
nyanganro suxni mshinikanuto nchinanro taluka gimtuwnaletmaka
xani goshpotu nkamrutanru nusanate gikeko chowgutyaplu nutakle
totu gigkaklewyegitanwu tye kayno pejnruneko
girukotkalurni wumane ma wyayixyapa
pejnurunekokta nomolene katslutewatatkana ga wa gitni gikeko
jimekapu ptaji tutjata nepuro giyampotuko tamanutana
mala mtashaya pejnuruneko jejine rumata chalugatna
pekakgitanro yimaklewatachro kamrurchi pyonanatanrutka tetjekamruretyapyi
petpotutanna koshichiwgene kiglerpotna gige panikanna satu penekanunno gitni
gatnugapo netyalo gimnumta wanekta twanata
noturu giwa gitakawalu shiji nenekyagi nsaletatkalu
pochwalu tkamrujetanrukaka teneksatwu nsaplo
nshicho gimugkaklewkakanu pganuruyma giwa gimtuwnashatanu
wuglepokotanutkalu psoluko gawyawaka nshicho kigle getle rixyawa wupji
wa yine gimwakaklewu giwa wayegixkaka pimrineyma
kamgaka mokawa koya rutagatyapna suxone maklojine
giwa kigleru wyanshinikanru nepuro wkagwakanna wganurune wepomganna rumenatyawakna
xani ginakakta tyotaljenatya nustaplole nuykotmakatkalo seyni giwa tjema
ganigapi shpatayma tuylakyanru suxo tganurni topjiya
pagixanu mnunanuka tanjimta nsaplo gikta teneksatanunno
rukshikamtanatkana kwangikleru weyiwakopshinna shiji chowginatnina
nwugenene gipxakananumtanro gyegwaklo tusanateya girixanu twenutangi
kgaylokleru chinruna wale makluji girixanu gixo suxonni yokwita pokchiya
tsru panchi kamruta nuru pejnuruneko gimolene gwiyawakapa
giwa nugleretlu nokanopi saglekaka nsatkakanru nanikanru
nyegwaklo pixanupje gimatune panikanu girixanu waneyatkano gita
xani giwa jemanunro nuru nyegwaklopni rumatjemanroge rurgognenatanu gawarinti
kapetgogne nyonatlu mkachrinama xani nushagkanutkalu satpacha nushagkinru
petashatanutkalu panchi waneko gixkalurpatkani wanepnute wugletanru
tugkakleyegpotutwu yimaklewatachro wumatjemyapa pejnuruneko jiglokachine
petanna tsroshkikine saxpatatkana mkachrisama kamrutyapna
giptogiykaka nkamrutanru katsluje ranokyaplu totu
xani wushinkapanru wjiglokjejenatyawaka xanikta pnuko rixatka
gishagkakalurnige mkachrikaka giyaka gigkakanno nagjityapa gitkoxa
penekanunwu jiweje wjiwetinripa pejnuruneko suxone
njirukotanru jimaprokaka ralixinpotunanukotka pejnuruko nkoshpakanru gnikyaplu
nyegwaklu gikshikamtlu satu yine gimetachrini gatnugapoya rumkanatana
pejnuruneko nomolene ginrikapa seyni natjirune gike
pugkakanno noturu katunni giynumapi gerotu nugleretlo
jiji muxojitu njitotana kapetgogne sanaya namanpotutana
pugkakanna wsalwayegityapna pasretga gwachine wumolene
nkamrurewatana pshinitsongogneji netapanro nshicho yayixachro
giwa pkojwakanshinikanutanu nunro kiglewu gawyawaka
rumata girukotnawana maklojine yimakletapkana kpinrewaklerone gatalaya gajene
ginakakta retinarona makloji gasuktatachro kashichanunrona solalone
rumuwatatka mturu pochwajiru rapikinitkalu ramikne
kamrurewatachine chanixkalune gapokatka tyegogne
gike parini wale makluji yotaljeshata ginakakokta yajeta giyagni gikeko nenekannatkalu
rapokatkana gixo konigone chiji rushinikamtna sana kamrutyapna
sotluji mtserkakatu tapatjeta najiro tugletyaplu gatnugapo
psoluko pagixankaka niikaluru tanjimta nunro wanepnutkoxa mkachri gerkakalurupa
pugkakanna pumolene giwakatanruna psoluko yokanatkalurupa gatalaya
nikaluru tyokanyejetlu tganuru namikne tumananusreta
giwa raluka gepomgaletluna gitsrukaachi pikluna girixanu ruwshokanunna kamrurchiya
runatka wutsrukate wkomjikjeru kshinikanurpotni giyagni wugleretlu
rapatanatanna yineru mshinikanutu seyni jemamtluna xani repomganunruna
jiglokyawakayna rutsolguwatna namanutanatka njemyawakna
giwa taluka genekletanro yoshkikagapi jiro nunroni tunanshichyanro
kiruka yonamtatkaluro reneksatwu pogirchi wuynumsatyaplu wtokanu
giwaka yonatinipa wane wetinri susawlepa gikta pixkakaklupni
tumata yantaletatka mturo pamyomyoji tyantajeta
giwa walekopixka rixpokotinitkana kanawa wa numwastsitanru pnuko rixatkalu
kapetogne tanika pagixagkaka nyegwaklo seyni gikeko teneklo nunro
gixo yine geta rasuktatyawakna mturune yenewatyawakna
xani rujruka pagixanutetanuna nepurni giwa rostupotutlu kostalmapa
wapatjetanutkalu pejnuruko wpagixanute nganuru kowgutanatkawuna
psusawotanru kiruksure pyagapgatinri chinanu nepuro
panchiko putukanu nshicho pugkakyaplu puru nkagapgatyawaka
xani galikaka retkoklunutkanutka motoro ranikanutkaluna kwangixlerune
gikeko teta nshicho girixanu yogimgimatna pejnuruneko yine
nyegwaklo  gijpanno nujrukana pyotunkakanunno
panchi nutakamtlu noturu wane rawgognenatinripa giwa yenewjetanu
yeye pyanshinikanutanu gigowukatkalu goyakalu pkegeknanuwatanuna
pochkepyi wjempotutanru chinyawakwu gitsrukachi
giwa raniklo rushicho gosi yagapgatyawaka girixanu tchiyagatanuna tunro tamtakanuna
gixo gopshi tpurata najiro kapetogne pamole tushagkapa garoso tagjityapa
kugleru gipxakaklu chinna rusanatewatinna wa yine gorowampa gajene
chalugatinipa kashpotutanru chalu ma rujrukyapa
giwa giylatanno gitkoxa galuka giwekleta nsaletanatkano
pnute rixanno nganuru rumtuwnakaknno kapetgogne
wpoyagkakanru wuxixini chinyawakwuna tsrune mawyayixyapa
puglajpotuta rugkakinyina nupniyawaka pguta nomole yokwitanyina
gitumkata kawleta makloji gimtugachro wenuya tyayixanxako
rushinikjetnirina gimolene wa sekontoni seyni xani ramtakanatkaluna ramgapotunatatka
kachinonno notjiya nyayixana gixo walapu wannixanatka
kiglerunwu gapoka gimka wyayixni giyagni wjirukotinwa
xani goctowre wyagapgatanu nganuruyma pokalpa pokchi gayanu
gepirutu tkoshpakana maklojni gipsochkokonanna
malnanwakataa nikgogletana klukta gimtuknanwakatanno
